 ) Social networking website Facebook has developed an automated service to protect the accounts of its consumers, which can detect stolen e-mail addresses and passwords through web monitoring
 yah seva upabhoktaaon se judi jaankariyon kii jaanch kar yah pataa lagaaegi ki yah fasebuk par istemaal kii janevaali jaankariyon se mail khaati he yaa nahin

 60 rupee prati litre or dijal par 30 paise prati litre kii vruddhi kii gai thi jisase 3,200 karod rupee kaa atirikt rajasav jutaya ja sake
 Thus, the excise duty on fuel has been hiked four times so far in the current financial year
 vahiin sarkaar ne 17 disambar, 2015 ko petrol par utpaada shulk 30 paise or dijal par 1
 17 per liter, to raise additional revenue of Rs 2,500 crore
 saat november, 2015 ko petrol par utpaada shulk main 1
 An increase of Rs 60 per liter and 30 paise per liter on diesel was made to raise additional revenue of Rs 3,200 crore
 is tarah chaalu vitt varsh main abhi tak eendhan par utpaada shulk main chaar baar badhotaree kii gai he

 alag alag guruon kii dhyaan paddati-osho(rajnish)- duniya main sabase saral or prachlit dhyaan kii vidhioshone bataai he- ise unhone "sakriy dhyaan" kaha he, jo paanch charnon main hota he- is dhyaan ko samooh main yaa akele karnaa hota he, parantu yah samooh main zyada prabhaavshaalee hota he- osho ne dhyaan kii anya vidhiyon ke bare main bhi bataaya he- armbh se lekar aage badhane tak kai seedhiyaan bataai gayi hai- osho ke dhyaan main rang, sugandh or nrity-sangeet par bhi vishesh jor diya gaya he- inke dhyaan or sadhana main chakron ko camel pushp ke saamaan bataaya gaya habuddha- vartmaan main jis vyakti ne ishwar ko dhyaan se paane kaa maarg bataaya , vah vyakti buddha hi the- buddha ne ashtaangyogke madhyam se dhyaan kaa maarg bataaya- buddha ne aacharan , vyavhaar or jivan darshan ke madhyam se ishwar kii uplabdhi ke liye kaary kiya- buddha ke dhyaan paddati main chakra , chakke kii tarah hote hai- buddha kii dhyaan paddati ab bahut sari paddatiyon main ghul mil gayi he- par mul rup se yah abhi lamaaon kii parampara main jivit haiyogaanand- paramhansayogaanandane dhyaan kii jis vidhi kaa duniya bhar main prachaar prasar kiya , vah he - kriya yoga- mul rup se kriya yoga paddati kaa avishkaar ek mahaan guru "baba ji maharaj" ne kiya tha- is paddati main bhi kai charnon ke baad hi dhyaan tak panhuchane kaa avasar miltaa he- kriya yoga paddati , tamaam dhyaan paddatiyon kaa anoothaa sanyog heanandamurti- anandamurti ji ne bahut sari dhyaan paddatiyon kaa srijan or vikaas kiya- shiv, krishna or buddha kii dhyaan paddatiyon ko dobaaraa jivit karne or unka samanvay karne kaa shrey anandamurti ji ko jaataa he- inhone sahaj yoga, vishesh yoga or madhur sadhana jaisi tamaam dhyaan paddatiyaan di hai- yahan par bhi chakra camel ke pushp kii tarah hi hai- yama - niyam ke saath inaki sadhana or dhyaan kii paddatiyaan vyakti ko bhautik or aadhyatmik uplabdhi , donon de sakati handhyaan karne main kya-kya saavdhaaniyaan rakhni chahie?- bina kisi aadhaar or uddeshy ke liye dhyaan na karen- jis vyakti se aapako dhyaan siikhnaa he, pehle uski uplabdhiyaan jaan len- dhyaan seekhney ke purv , us vyakti kaa jivan or saamaajik darshan jaanane kaa prayaas karen- keval aakarshan ke liye dhyaan kii ore na jaaen- ek raste par hi chalem , baar baar tareekon main badlaav na karen- yaad rakhiye, keval aankh band karnaa dhyaan nahin hota, or dhyaan hota nahin, ghat jaataa he During the Lok Sabha elections, employment opportunities have increased in the country

 ' Urmila Shirish is one of the most important storytellers of our times

 ) The Supreme Court said that if a person accepts the post of minister, then he cannot use the right of freedom of speech of ordinary citizen in that way

 supreme court ne is sambandh main sanket diya he

 maamle kii agali sunwaayee 2 may ko he
 In Bulandshahar, the Supreme Court is hearing an important hearing in the mother-daughter gang rape case
 pichhali sunwaayee main mahilaon se rape ke maamle main ohade par baithe shaks dwaara bayaanbaji par supreme court ne bade sanvaidhanik sawaal uthaae the ki The constitution of the country has given women equal rights, separate identities and rights to live dignified life
 aise main kisi rape peedit mahila ke khilaaf ohade par baithe vyakti kii bayaanbaji kya mahila ke garimapurna jivan ke adhikaar ko thes nahin pahunchaati
 Can a person sitting in a public office call a serious crime like rape a political conspiracy? Is the victim not violating the free and fair trial of the woman's constitution as it may affect the investigation
 samvidhan dwaara diya gaya koi bhi moulik adhikaar sampurna nahin kyonki ye kanoon niyantrit he
 In such a situation, no person can say that in cases like rape, such rhetoric comes under the fundamental right to speak
 yahaan maamla sirf kisi kii bolne kii aazaadee kaa adhikaar kaa nahin balki peedita ke kanoon ke samaksh samaan sangrakshan or free and fere trial ke adhikaar kaa bhi he
 If the accused says that he has been implicated under the conspiracy then the matter is different but if a DGP says that the victim is false then what will the police investigate the matter? The question here is that if the person on the position is rhetorical in this way, even if a crime It is not within the scope of, but it also comes under the purview of morality and etiquette given in the Constitution
 vahiin, centre sarkaar kii ore se iskaa virodh kiya gaya
 AG Mukul Rohatgi said there is no law regarding this
 is tarah court moral code of conduct nahin bana saktaa
 However, if someone makes such a statement, then the trial court can take action against him
 supreme court ne is maamle main fali nariman ke saath saath harish salve ko bhi court kii sahyog karne ko kaha he

 Any fundamental right given by the constitution is not absolute because this law is governed
 aise main koi bhi shaks ye nahin kah saktaa he rape jaise maamalon main aisi bayaanbaji bolne ke adhikaar ke moulik adhikaar ke daayre main aata he
